name:B‚Äçe‚Äç-‚ÄçP‚Äçe‚Äç-‚Äçn‚Äçe‚Äçu‚Äçn
info:Queen Room With Garden View
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Couples
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 24, 2023
msg:Wellness and feel good oasis in Shenyang 

We combined it with a night in the hotel. 
Underground parking. 
The big building is the spa. It‚Äôs not easy to miss. 
The check-in is not in the big Spa Building. Overnighters have to go to the building next door, following the ‚Äûcheck-in signs‚Äú. 
There they inform you that:
- The day of check in you can use the Spa area until 10 pm. 
- Day of checkout a delicious breakfast with much variety of cooked and fresh dishes, fruits, juices and coffee and sweets is served from 7-10am. 
- If you check out before 10 am you can use the Spa area again until 6pm that day. 
- To enter the Spa area you need to go to the big building. You need to let them know your room number and they need your passport / ID card. 
- You will get a number for your individual locker. If you are a couple check the ticket with number for sign of female or male. 
- You take off your shoes, exchange them for slippers they offer and store your shoes in your locker. You get a key you take inside which is for free. 
- You will be led into gender separated changing areas. 
- You get a free towel, lounge shirt and shirt pants to change in and sign for it with your key. There is staff to show you how. 
- Your key shows your number and area in which your individual locker is located in. There is staff to show you how. 
- Inside you first pass a gender separated area. Here you can be naked. 
- Then you can leave that area and join the gender mixed area. 
- It has 4 levels with indoor and outdoor pools and hot tubs. 
- Level 1 has outdoor pools, indoor pools, whirlpools, children‚Äôs water park and access to the wave park, which opens 4x a day for half an hour. 
- Level 2 is more quiet with healthier whirlpool options. 
- Level 3  has sauna houses for free open until 10pm, a movie theatre, KTV, food area and a children play area all open until 9:30pm. 
- Level 4 is for private treatments. 
In winter the outdoor waterpark/slides ‚Äûthe wave‚Äú and terrace pools are closed due to the cold. 
We were surprised of how relaxing the stay at the Spa was. There is many people but the Spa building is amazingly huge and has many different areas to lay down and corners in which it was very peaceful. 

Our hotel room ‚ÄûRoom Queensize-Bed‚Äú was lovely and the staff very attentive. We ordered ice-cubes, extra water and had pizza delivered to the hotel. 
All in all, a wonderful experience, which we will repeat.
